<s> tunstal who was in the prince's service was twice or thrice in and out of our camp the french in theirs of arlieu and about arras <\s>
<s> a little river the canihe i think twas called but this is writ away from books and europe and the only map the writer hath of these scenes of his youth bears no mark of this little stream divided our pickets from the enemy's <\s>
<s> our sentries talked across the stream when they could make themselves understood to each other and when they could not grinned and handed each other their brandy flasks or their pouches of tobacco <\s>
<s> and one fine day of june riding thither with the officer who visited the outposts colonel esmond was taking an airing on horseback being too weak for military duty they came to this river where a number of english and scots were assembled talking to the good natured enemy on the other side <\s>
<s> esmond was especially amused with the talk of one long fellow with a great curling red moustache and blue eyes that was half a dozen inches taller than his swarthy little comrades on the french side of the stream and being asked by the colonel saluted him and said that he belonged to the royal cravats <\s>
<s> from his way of saying royal cravat esmond at once knew that the fellow's tongue had first wagged on the banks of the liffey and not the loire and the poor soldier a deserter probably did not like to venture very deep into french conversation lest his unlucky brogue should peep out <\s>
<s> he chose to restrict himself to such few expressions in the french language as he thought he had mastered easily and his attempt at disguise was infinitely amusing <\s>
<s> esmond whistled lillibullero at which teague's eyes began to twinkle and then flung him a dollar when the poor boy broke out with a god bless that is dieu benisse votre honor that would infallibly have sent him to the provost marshal had he been on our side of the river <\s>
<s> whilst this parley was going on three officers on horseback on the french side appeared at some little distance and stopped as if eying us when one of them left the other two and rode close up to us who were by the stream <\s>
<s> says the royal cravat with great agitation pas lui that's he not him l'autre and pointed to the distant officer on a chestnut horse with a cuirass shining in the sun and over it a broad blue ribbon <\s>
<s> please to take mr <\s>
<s> hamilton's services to my lord marlborough my lord duke says the gentleman in english and looking to see that the party were not hostilely disposed he added with a smile there's a friend of yours gentlemen yonder he bids me to say that he saw some of your faces on the 11th of september last year <\s>
<s> as the gentleman spoke the other two officers rode up and came quite close <\s>
<s> we knew at once who it was <\s>
<s> it was the king then two and twenty years old tall and slim with deep brown eyes that looked melancholy though his lips wore a smile <\s>
<s> we took off our hats and saluted him <\s>
<s> no man sure could see for the first time without emotion the youthful inheritor of so much fame and misfortune <\s>
<s> it seemed to mr <\s>
<s> esmond that the prince was not unlike young castlewood whose age and figure he resembled <\s>
<s> the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george acknowledged the salute and looked at us hard <\s>
<s> even the idlers on our side of the river set up a hurrah <\s>
<s> as for the royal cravat he ran to the prince's stirrup knelt down and kissed his boot and bawled and looked a hundred ejaculations and blessings <\s>
<s> the prince bade the aide de camp give him a piece of money and when the party saluting us had ridden away cravat spat upon the piece of gold by way of benediction and swaggered away pouching his coin and twirling his honest carroty moustache <\s>
<s> the officer in whose company esmond was the same little captain of handyside's regiment mr <\s>
<s> sterne who had proposed the garden at lille when my lord mohun and esmond had their affair was an irishman too and as brave a little soul as ever wore a sword <\s>
<s> bedad says roger sterne that long fellow spoke french so beautiful that i shouldn't have known he wasn't a foreigner till he broke out with his hulla ballooing and only an irish calf can bellow like that <\s>
<s> and roger made another remark in his wild way in which there was sense as well as absurdity if that young gentleman says he would but ride over to our camp instead of villars's toss up his hat and say here am i the king who'll follow me <\s>
<s> by the lord esmond the whole army would rise and carry him home again and beat villars and take paris by the way <\s>
<s> the news of the prince's visit was all through the camp quickly and scores of ours went down in hopes to see him <\s>
<s> major hamilton whom we had talked with sent back by a trumpet several silver pieces for officers with us <\s>
<s> esmond received one of these and that medal and a recompense not uncommon amongst princes were the only rewards he ever had from a royal person whom he endeavored not very long after to serve <\s>
<s> esmond quitted the army almost immediately after this following his general home and indeed being advised to travel in the fine weather and attempt to take no further part in the campaign <\s>
<s> but he heard from the army that of the many who crowded to see the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george frank castlewood had made himself most conspicuous my lord viscount riding across the little stream bareheaded to where the prince was and dismounting and kneeling before him to do him homage <\s>
<s> some said that the prince had actually knighted him but my lord denied that statement though he acknowledged the rest of the story and said from having been out of favor with corporal john as he called the duke before his grace warned him not to commit those follies and smiled on him cordially ever after <\s>
<s> and he was so kind to me frank writ that i thought i would put in a good word for master harry but when i mentioned your name he looked as black as thunder and said he had never heard of you <\s>
<s> i go home and harp on the old string <\s>
<s> after quitting mons and the army and as he was waiting for a packet at ostend esmond had a letter from his young kinsman castlewood at bruxelles conveying intelligence whereof frank besought him to be the bearer to london and which caused colonel esmond no small anxiety <\s>
<s> the young scapegrace being one and twenty years old and being anxious to sow his wild otes as he wrote had married mademoiselle de wertheim daughter of count de wertheim chamberlain to the emperor and having a post in the household of the governor of the netherlands <\s>
<s> p s the young gentleman wrote clotilda is older than me which perhaps may be objected to her but i am so old a raik that the age makes no difference and i am determined to reform <\s>

<s> gudule by father holt <\s>
<s> she is heart and soul for the good cause <\s>

<s> she is a fair beauty <\s>

<s> so frank had married a roman catholic lady and an heir was expected and mr <\s>
<s> esmond was to carry this intelligence to his mistress at london <\s>
<s> twas a difficult embassy and the colonel felt not a little tremor as he neared the capital <\s>
<s> he reached his inn late and sent a messenger to kensington to announce his arrival and visit the next morning <\s>
<s> the messenger brought back news that the court was at windsor and the fair beatrix absent and engaged in her duties there <\s>
<s> only esmond's mistress remained in her house at kensington <\s>
<s> she appeared in court but once in the year beatrix was quite the mistress and ruler of the little mansion inviting the company thither and engaging in every conceivable frolic of town pleasure <\s>
<s> whilst her mother acting as the young lady's protectress and elder sister pursued her own path which was quite modest and secluded <\s>
<s> as soon as ever esmond was dressed and he had been awake long before the town he took a coach for kensington and reached it so early that he met his dear mistress coming home from morning prayers <\s>
<s> she carried her prayer book never allowing a footman to bear it as everybody else did and it was by this simple sign esmond knew what her occupation had been <\s>
<s> he called to the coachman to stop and jumped out as she looked towards him <\s>
<s> she wore her hood as usual and she turned quite pale when she saw him <\s>
<s> to feel that kind little hand near to his heart seemed to give him strength <\s>
<s> they were soon at the door of her ladyship's house and within it <\s>
<s> with a sweet sad smile she took his hand and kissed it <\s>
<s> how ill you have been how weak you look my dear henry she said <\s>
<s> tis certain the colonel did look like a ghost except that ghosts do not look very happy tis said <\s>
<s> esmond always felt so on returning to her after absence indeed whenever he looked in her sweet kind face <\s>
<s> i am come back to be nursed by my family says he <\s>
<s> if frank had not taken care of me after my wound very likely i should have gone altogether <\s>

<s> esmond received one of these and that medal and a recompense not uncommon amongst princes were the only rewards he ever had from a royal person whom he endeavored not very long after to serve <\s>
<s> esmond quitted the army almost immediately after this following his general home and indeed being advised to travel in the fine weather and attempt to take no further part in the campaign <\s>
<s> but he heard from the army that of the many who crowded to see the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george frank castlewood had made himself most conspicuous my lord viscount riding across the little stream bareheaded to where the prince was and dismounting and kneeling before him to do him homage <\s>
<s> some said that the prince had actually knighted him but my lord denied that statement though he acknowledged the rest of the story and said from having been out of favor with corporal john as he called the duke before his grace warned him not to commit those follies and smiled on him cordially ever after <\s>
<s> and he was so kind to me frank writ that i thought i would put in a good word for master harry but when i mentioned your name he looked as black as thunder and said he had never heard of you <\s>
<s> i go home and harp on the old string <\s>
<s> after quitting mons and the army and as he was waiting for a packet at ostend esmond had a letter from his young kinsman castlewood at bruxelles conveying intelligence whereof frank besought him to be the bearer to london and which caused colonel esmond no small anxiety <\s>
<s> the young scapegrace being one and twenty years old and being anxious to sow his wild otes as he wrote had married mademoiselle de wertheim daughter of count de wertheim chamberlain to the emperor and having a post in the household of the governor of the netherlands <\s>
<s> p s the young gentleman wrote clotilda is older than me which perhaps may be objected to her but i am so old a raik that the age makes no difference and i am determined to reform <\s>
<s> we were married at st <\s>
<s> gudule by father holt <\s>
<s> she is heart and soul for the good cause <\s>
<s> and here the cry is vif le roy which my mother will join in and trix too <\s>
<s> break this news to em gently and tell mr <\s>
<s> finch my agent to press the people for their rents and send me the ryno anyhow <\s>
<s> clotilda sings and plays on the spinet beautifully <\s>
<s> she is a fair beauty <\s>
<s> and if it's a son you shall stand godfather <\s>
<s> i'm going to leave the army having had enuf of soldering and my lord duke recommends me <\s>
<s> i shall pass the winter here and stop at least until clo's lying in <\s>
<s> i call her old clo but nobody else shall <\s>
<s> she is the cleverest woman in all bruxelles understanding painting music poetry and perfect at cookery and puddens <\s>
<s> i borded with the count that's how i came to know her <\s>
<s> there are four counts her brothers <\s>
<s> one an abbey three with the prince's army <\s>
<s> they have a lawsuit for an immence fortune but are now in a pore way <\s>
<s> break this to mother who'll take anything from you <\s>
<s> and write and bid finch write amediately <\s>
<s> hostel de l'aigle noire bruxelles flanders <\s>
<s> so frank had married a roman catholic lady and an heir was expected and mr <\s>
<s> esmond was to carry this intelligence to his mistress at london <\s>
<s> twas a difficult embassy and the colonel felt not a little tremor as he neared the capital <\s>
<s> he reached his inn late and sent a messenger to kensington to announce his arrival and visit the next morning <\s>
<s> the messenger brought back news that the court was at windsor and the fair beatrix absent and engaged in her duties there <\s>
<s> only esmond's mistress remained in her house at kensington <\s>
<s> she appeared in court but once in the year beatrix was quite the mistress and ruler of the little mansion inviting the company thither and engaging in every conceivable frolic of town pleasure <\s>
<s> whilst her mother acting as the young lady's protectress and elder sister pursued her own path which was quite modest and secluded <\s>
<s> as soon as ever esmond was dressed and he had been awake long before the town he took a coach for kensington and reached it so early that he met his dear mistress coming home from morning prayers <\s>
<s> she carried her prayer book never allowing a footman to bear it as everybody else did and it was by this simple sign esmond knew what her occupation had been <\s>
<s> he called to the coachman to stop and jumped out as she looked towards him <\s>
<s> she wore her hood as usual and she turned quite pale when she saw him <\s>
<s> to feel that kind little hand near to his heart seemed to give him strength <\s>
<s> they were soon at the door of her ladyship's house and within it <\s>
<s> with a sweet sad smile she took his hand and kissed it <\s>
<s> how ill you have been how weak you look my dear henry she said <\s>
<s> tis certain the colonel did look like a ghost except that ghosts do not look very happy tis said <\s>
<s> esmond always felt so on returning to her after absence indeed whenever he looked in her sweet kind face <\s>
<s> i am come back to be nursed by my family says he <\s>
<s> if frank had not taken care of me after my wound very likely i should have gone altogether <\s>
<s> poor frank good frank <\s>
<s> you'll always be kind to him my lord she went on <\s>
<s> the poor child never knew he was doing you a wrong <\s>
<s> cries out colonel esmond <\s>
<s> what do you mean dear lady <\s>
<s> i am no lady says she i am rachel esmond francis esmond's widow my lord <\s>
<s> i cannot bear that title <\s>
<s> would we never had taken it from him who has it now <\s>
<s> but we did all in our power henry we did all in our power and my lord and i that is who told you this tale dearest lady <\s>
<s> have you not had the letter i writ you <\s>
<s> i writ to you at mons directly i heard it says lady esmond <\s>
<s> he was come back a greater jacobite than ever and esmond suspected that some fair conspirators at bruxelles had been inflaming the young man's ardor <\s>
<s> indeed he owned that he had a message from the queen beatrix's godmother who had given her name to frank's sister the year before he and his sovereign were born <\s>
<s> however desirous marshal villars might be to fight my lord duke did not seem disposed to indulge him this campaign <\s>
<s> last year his grace had been all for the whigs and hanoverians but finding on going to england his country cold towards himself and the people in a ferment of high church loyalty the duke comes back to his army cooled towards the hanoverians cautious with the imperialists and particularly civil and polite towards the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> tis certain that messengers and letters were continually passing between his grace and his brave nephew the duke of berwick in the opposite camp <\s>
<s> no man's caresses were more opportune than his grace's and no man ever uttered expressions of regard and affection more generously <\s>
<s> he professed to monsieur de torcy so mr <\s>
<s> john told the writer quite an eagerness to be cut in pieces for the exiled queen and her family nay more i believe this year he parted with a portion of the most precious part of himself his money which he sent over to the royal exiles <\s>
<s> tunstal who was in the prince's service was twice or thrice in and out of our camp the french in theirs of arlieu and about arras <\s>
<s> a little river the canihe i think twas called but this is writ away from books and europe and the only map the writer hath of these scenes of his youth bears no mark of this little stream divided our pickets from the enemy's <\s>
<s> our sentries talked across the stream when they could make themselves understood to each other and when they could not grinned and handed each other their brandy flasks or their pouches of tobacco <\s>
<s> and one fine day of june riding thither with the officer who visited the outposts colonel esmond was taking an airing on horseback being too weak for military duty they came to this river where a number of english and scots were assembled talking to the good natured enemy on the other side <\s>
<s> esmond was especially amused with the talk of one long fellow with a great curling red moustache and blue eyes that was half a dozen inches taller than his swarthy little comrades on the french side of the stream and being asked by the colonel saluted him and said that he belonged to the royal cravats <\s>
<s> from his way of saying royal cravat esmond at once knew that the fellow's tongue had first wagged on the banks of the liffey and not the loire and the poor soldier a deserter probably did not like to venture very deep into french conversation lest his unlucky brogue should peep out <\s>
<s> he chose to restrict himself to such few expressions in the french language as he thought he had mastered easily and his attempt at disguise was infinitely amusing <\s>
<s> esmond whistled lillibullero at which teague's eyes began to twinkle and then flung him a dollar when the poor boy broke out with a god bless that is dieu benisse votre honor that would infallibly have sent him to the provost marshal had he been on our side of the river <\s>
<s> whilst this parley was going on three officers on horseback on the french side appeared at some little distance and stopped as if eying us when one of them left the other two and rode close up to us who were by the stream <\s>
<s> says the royal cravat with great agitation pas lui that's he not him l'autre and pointed to the distant officer on a chestnut horse with a cuirass shining in the sun and over it a broad blue ribbon <\s>
<s> please to take mr <\s>
<s> hamilton's services to my lord marlborough my lord duke says the gentleman in english and looking to see that the party were not hostilely disposed he added with a smile there's a friend of yours gentlemen yonder he bids me to say that he saw some of your faces on the 11th of september last year <\s>
<s> as the gentleman spoke the other two officers rode up and came quite close <\s>
<s> we knew at once who it was <\s>
<s> it was the king then two and twenty years old tall and slim with deep brown eyes that looked melancholy though his lips wore a smile <\s>
<s> we took off our hats and saluted him <\s>
<s> no man sure could see for the first time without emotion the youthful inheritor of so much fame and misfortune <\s>
<s> it seemed to mr <\s>
<s> esmond that the prince was not unlike young castlewood whose age and figure he resembled <\s>
<s> the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george acknowledged the salute and looked at us hard <\s>
<s> even the idlers on our side of the river set up a hurrah <\s>

<s> the prince bade the aide de camp give him a piece of money and when the party saluting us had ridden away cravat spat upon the piece of gold by way of benediction and swaggered away pouching his coin and twirling his honest carroty moustache <\s>
<s> the officer in whose company esmond was the same little captain of handyside's regiment mr <\s>

<s> he was come back a greater jacobite than ever and esmond suspected that some fair conspirators at bruxelles had been inflaming the young man's ardor <\s>
<s> indeed he owned that he had a message from the queen beatrix's godmother who had given her name to frank's sister the year before he and his sovereign were born <\s>
<s> however desirous marshal villars might be to fight my lord duke did not seem disposed to indulge him this campaign <\s>
<s> last year his grace had been all for the whigs and hanoverians but finding on going to england his country cold towards himself and the people in a ferment of high church loyalty the duke comes back to his army cooled towards the hanoverians cautious with the imperialists and particularly civil and polite towards the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> tis certain that messengers and letters were continually passing between his grace and his brave nephew the duke of berwick in the opposite camp <\s>
<s> no man's caresses were more opportune than his grace's and no man ever uttered expressions of regard and affection more generously <\s>
<s> he professed to monsieur de torcy so mr <\s>
<s> john told the writer quite an eagerness to be cut in pieces for the exiled queen and her family nay more i believe this year he parted with a portion of the most precious part of himself his money which he sent over to the royal exiles <\s>
<s> tunstal who was in the prince's service was twice or thrice in and out of our camp the french in theirs of arlieu and about arras <\s>
<s> a little river the canihe i think twas called but this is writ away from books and europe and the only map the writer hath of these scenes of his youth bears no mark of this little stream divided our pickets from the enemy's <\s>
<s> our sentries talked across the stream when they could make themselves understood to each other and when they could not grinned and handed each other their brandy flasks or their pouches of tobacco <\s>
<s> and one fine day of june riding thither with the officer who visited the outposts colonel esmond was taking an airing on horseback being too weak for military duty they came to this river where a number of english and scots were assembled talking to the good natured enemy on the other side <\s>
<s> esmond was especially amused with the talk of one long fellow with a great curling red moustache and blue eyes that was half a dozen inches taller than his swarthy little comrades on the french side of the stream and being asked by the colonel saluted him and said that he belonged to the royal cravats <\s>
<s> from his way of saying royal cravat esmond at once knew that the fellow's tongue had first wagged on the banks of the liffey and not the loire and the poor soldier a deserter probably did not like to venture very deep into french conversation lest his unlucky brogue should peep out <\s>
<s> he chose to restrict himself to such few expressions in the french language as he thought he had mastered easily and his attempt at disguise was infinitely amusing <\s>
<s> esmond whistled lillibullero at which teague's eyes began to twinkle and then flung him a dollar when the poor boy broke out with a god bless that is dieu benisse votre honor that would infallibly have sent him to the provost marshal had he been on our side of the river <\s>
<s> whilst this parley was going on three officers on horseback on the french side appeared at some little distance and stopped as if eying us when one of them left the other two and rode close up to us who were by the stream <\s>
<s> says the royal cravat with great agitation pas lui that's he not him l'autre and pointed to the distant officer on a chestnut horse with a cuirass shining in the sun and over it a broad blue ribbon <\s>
<s> please to take mr <\s>
<s> hamilton's services to my lord marlborough my lord duke says the gentleman in english and looking to see that the party were not hostilely disposed he added with a smile there's a friend of yours gentlemen yonder he bids me to say that he saw some of your faces on the 11th of september last year <\s>
<s> as the gentleman spoke the other two officers rode up and came quite close <\s>
<s> we knew at once who it was <\s>
<s> it was the king then two and twenty years old tall and slim with deep brown eyes that looked melancholy though his lips wore a smile <\s>
<s> we took off our hats and saluted him <\s>
<s> no man sure could see for the first time without emotion the youthful inheritor of so much fame and misfortune <\s>
<s> it seemed to mr <\s>
<s> esmond that the prince was not unlike young castlewood whose age and figure he resembled <\s>
<s> the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george acknowledged the salute and looked at us hard <\s>
<s> even the idlers on our side of the river set up a hurrah <\s>
<s> as for the royal cravat he ran to the prince's stirrup knelt down and kissed his boot and bawled and looked a hundred ejaculations and blessings <\s>
<s> the prince bade the aide de camp give him a piece of money and when the party saluting us had ridden away cravat spat upon the piece of gold by way of benediction and swaggered away pouching his coin and twirling his honest carroty moustache <\s>
<s> the officer in whose company esmond was the same little captain of handyside's regiment mr <\s>
<s> sterne who had proposed the garden at lille when my lord mohun and esmond had their affair was an irishman too and as brave a little soul as ever wore a sword <\s>
<s> bedad says roger sterne that long fellow spoke french so beautiful that i shouldn't have known he wasn't a foreigner till he broke out with his hulla ballooing and only an irish calf can bellow like that <\s>
<s> and roger made another remark in his wild way in which there was sense as well as absurdity if that young gentleman says he would but ride over to our camp instead of villars's toss up his hat and say here am i the king who'll follow me <\s>
<s> by the lord esmond the whole army would rise and carry him home again and beat villars and take paris by the way <\s>
<s> the news of the prince's visit was all through the camp quickly and scores of ours went down in hopes to see him <\s>
<s> major hamilton whom we had talked with sent back by a trumpet several silver pieces for officers with us <\s>
<s> esmond received one of these and that medal and a recompense not uncommon amongst princes were the only rewards he ever had from a royal person whom he endeavored not very long after to serve <\s>
<s> esmond quitted the army almost immediately after this following his general home and indeed being advised to travel in the fine weather and attempt to take no further part in the campaign <\s>
<s> but he heard from the army that of the many who crowded to see the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george frank castlewood had made himself most conspicuous my lord viscount riding across the little stream bareheaded to where the prince was and dismounting and kneeling before him to do him homage <\s>
<s> some said that the prince had actually knighted him but my lord denied that statement though he acknowledged the rest of the story and said from having been out of favor with corporal john as he called the duke before his grace warned him not to commit those follies and smiled on him cordially ever after <\s>
<s> and he was so kind to me frank writ that i thought i would put in a good word for master harry but when i mentioned your name he looked as black as thunder and said he had never heard of you <\s>
<s> i go home and harp on the old string <\s>

<s> please to take mr <\s>
<s> hamilton's services to my lord marlborough my lord duke says the gentleman in english and looking to see that the party were not hostilely disposed he added with a smile there's a friend of yours gentlemen yonder he bids me to say that he saw some of your faces on the 11th of september last year <\s>
<s> as the gentleman spoke the other two officers rode up and came quite close <\s>
<s> we knew at once who it was <\s>
<s> it was the king then two and twenty years old tall and slim with deep brown eyes that looked melancholy though his lips wore a smile <\s>
<s> we took off our hats and saluted him <\s>
<s> no man sure could see for the first time without emotion the youthful inheritor of so much fame and misfortune <\s>
<s> it seemed to mr <\s>
<s> esmond that the prince was not unlike young castlewood whose age and figure he resembled <\s>
<s> the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george acknowledged the salute and looked at us hard <\s>
<s> even the idlers on our side of the river set up a hurrah <\s>
<s> as for the royal cravat he ran to the prince's stirrup knelt down and kissed his boot and bawled and looked a hundred ejaculations and blessings <\s>
<s> the prince bade the aide de camp give him a piece of money and when the party saluting us had ridden away cravat spat upon the piece of gold by way of benediction and swaggered away pouching his coin and twirling his honest carroty moustache <\s>
<s> the officer in whose company esmond was the same little captain of handyside's regiment mr <\s>
<s> sterne who had proposed the garden at lille when my lord mohun and esmond had their affair was an irishman too and as brave a little soul as ever wore a sword <\s>
<s> bedad says roger sterne that long fellow spoke french so beautiful that i shouldn't have known he wasn't a foreigner till he broke out with his hulla ballooing and only an irish calf can bellow like that <\s>
<s> and roger made another remark in his wild way in which there was sense as well as absurdity if that young gentleman says he would but ride over to our camp instead of villars's toss up his hat and say here am i the king who'll follow me <\s>
<s> by the lord esmond the whole army would rise and carry him home again and beat villars and take paris by the way <\s>
<s> the news of the prince's visit was all through the camp quickly and scores of ours went down in hopes to see him <\s>
<s> major hamilton whom we had talked with sent back by a trumpet several silver pieces for officers with us <\s>
<s> esmond received one of these and that medal and a recompense not uncommon amongst princes were the only rewards he ever had from a royal person whom he endeavored not very long after to serve <\s>
<s> esmond quitted the army almost immediately after this following his general home and indeed being advised to travel in the fine weather and attempt to take no further part in the campaign <\s>
<s> but he heard from the army that of the many who crowded to see the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george frank castlewood had made himself most conspicuous my lord viscount riding across the little stream bareheaded to where the prince was and dismounting and kneeling before him to do him homage <\s>
<s> some said that the prince had actually knighted him but my lord denied that statement though he acknowledged the rest of the story and said from having been out of favor with corporal john as he called the duke before his grace warned him not to commit those follies and smiled on him cordially ever after <\s>
<s> and he was so kind to me frank writ that i thought i would put in a good word for master harry but when i mentioned your name he looked as black as thunder and said he had never heard of you <\s>
<s> i go home and harp on the old string <\s>
<s> after quitting mons and the army and as he was waiting for a packet at ostend esmond had a letter from his young kinsman castlewood at bruxelles conveying intelligence whereof frank besought him to be the bearer to london and which caused colonel esmond no small anxiety <\s>
<s> the young scapegrace being one and twenty years old and being anxious to sow his wild otes as he wrote had married mademoiselle de wertheim daughter of count de wertheim chamberlain to the emperor and having a post in the household of the governor of the netherlands <\s>
<s> p s the young gentleman wrote clotilda is older than me which perhaps may be objected to her but i am so old a raik that the age makes no difference and i am determined to reform <\s>
<s> we were married at st <\s>
<s> gudule by father holt <\s>
<s> she is heart and soul for the good cause <\s>

<s> finch my agent to press the people for their rents and send me the ryno anyhow <\s>

<s> she is a fair beauty <\s>

<s> hostel de l'aigle noire bruxelles flanders <\s>
<s> so frank had married a roman catholic lady and an heir was expected and mr <\s>
<s> esmond was to carry this intelligence to his mistress at london <\s>
<s> twas a difficult embassy and the colonel felt not a little tremor as he neared the capital <\s>
<s> he reached his inn late and sent a messenger to kensington to announce his arrival and visit the next morning <\s>
<s> the messenger brought back news that the court was at windsor and the fair beatrix absent and engaged in her duties there <\s>
<s> only esmond's mistress remained in her house at kensington <\s>
<s> she appeared in court but once in the year beatrix was quite the mistress and ruler of the little mansion inviting the company thither and engaging in every conceivable frolic of town pleasure <\s>
<s> whilst her mother acting as the young lady's protectress and elder sister pursued her own path which was quite modest and secluded <\s>
<s> as soon as ever esmond was dressed and he had been awake long before the town he took a coach for kensington and reached it so early that he met his dear mistress coming home from morning prayers <\s>
<s> she carried her prayer book never allowing a footman to bear it as everybody else did and it was by this simple sign esmond knew what her occupation had been <\s>
<s> he called to the coachman to stop and jumped out as she looked towards him <\s>
<s> she wore her hood as usual and she turned quite pale when she saw him <\s>
<s> to feel that kind little hand near to his heart seemed to give him strength <\s>
<s> they were soon at the door of her ladyship's house and within it <\s>
<s> with a sweet sad smile she took his hand and kissed it <\s>
<s> how ill you have been how weak you look my dear henry she said <\s>
<s> tis certain the colonel did look like a ghost except that ghosts do not look very happy tis said <\s>
<s> esmond always felt so on returning to her after absence indeed whenever he looked in her sweet kind face <\s>
<s> i am come back to be nursed by my family says he <\s>
<s> if frank had not taken care of me after my wound very likely i should have gone altogether <\s>
<s> poor frank good frank <\s>
<s> you'll always be kind to him my lord she went on <\s>
<s> the poor child never knew he was doing you a wrong <\s>
<s> cries out colonel esmond <\s>

<s> he was come back a greater jacobite than ever and esmond suspected that some fair conspirators at bruxelles had been inflaming the young man's ardor <\s>
<s> indeed he owned that he had a message from the queen beatrix's godmother who had given her name to frank's sister the year before he and his sovereign were born <\s>
<s> however desirous marshal villars might be to fight my lord duke did not seem disposed to indulge him this campaign <\s>
<s> last year his grace had been all for the whigs and hanoverians but finding on going to england his country cold towards himself and the people in a ferment of high church loyalty the duke comes back to his army cooled towards the hanoverians cautious with the imperialists and particularly civil and polite towards the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> tis certain that messengers and letters were continually passing between his grace and his brave nephew the duke of berwick in the opposite camp <\s>

<s> and one fine day of june riding thither with the officer who visited the outposts colonel esmond was taking an airing on horseback being too weak for military duty they came to this river where a number of english and scots were assembled talking to the good natured enemy on the other side <\s>
<s> esmond was especially amused with the talk of one long fellow with a great curling red moustache and blue eyes that was half a dozen inches taller than his swarthy little comrades on the french side of the stream and being asked by the colonel saluted him and said that he belonged to the royal cravats <\s>

<s> the messenger brought back news that the court was at windsor and the fair beatrix absent and engaged in her duties there <\s>
<s> only esmond's mistress remained in her house at kensington <\s>
<s> she appeared in court but once in the year beatrix was quite the mistress and ruler of the little mansion inviting the company thither and engaging in every conceivable frolic of town pleasure <\s>
<s> whilst her mother acting as the young lady's protectress and elder sister pursued her own path which was quite modest and secluded <\s>
<s> as soon as ever esmond was dressed and he had been awake long before the town he took a coach for kensington and reached it so early that he met his dear mistress coming home from morning prayers <\s>
<s> she carried her prayer book never allowing a footman to bear it as everybody else did and it was by this simple sign esmond knew what her occupation had been <\s>
<s> he called to the coachman to stop and jumped out as she looked towards him <\s>
<s> she wore her hood as usual and she turned quite pale when she saw him <\s>
<s> to feel that kind little hand near to his heart seemed to give him strength <\s>
<s> they were soon at the door of her ladyship's house and within it <\s>
<s> with a sweet sad smile she took his hand and kissed it <\s>

<s> he was come back a greater jacobite than ever and esmond suspected that some fair conspirators at bruxelles had been inflaming the young man's ardor <\s>
<s> indeed he owned that he had a message from the queen beatrix's godmother who had given her name to frank's sister the year before he and his sovereign were born <\s>
<s> however desirous marshal villars might be to fight my lord duke did not seem disposed to indulge him this campaign <\s>
<s> last year his grace had been all for the whigs and hanoverians but finding on going to england his country cold towards himself and the people in a ferment of high church loyalty the duke comes back to his army cooled towards the hanoverians cautious with the imperialists and particularly civil and polite towards the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> tis certain that messengers and letters were continually passing between his grace and his brave nephew the duke of berwick in the opposite camp <\s>
<s> no man's caresses were more opportune than his grace's and no man ever uttered expressions of regard and affection more generously <\s>
<s> he professed to monsieur de torcy so mr <\s>
<s> john told the writer quite an eagerness to be cut in pieces for the exiled queen and her family nay more i believe this year he parted with a portion of the most precious part of himself his money which he sent over to the royal exiles <\s>
<s> tunstal who was in the prince's service was twice or thrice in and out of our camp the french in theirs of arlieu and about arras <\s>
<s> a little river the canihe i think twas called but this is writ away from books and europe and the only map the writer hath of these scenes of his youth bears no mark of this little stream divided our pickets from the enemy's <\s>
<s> our sentries talked across the stream when they could make themselves understood to each other and when they could not grinned and handed each other their brandy flasks or their pouches of tobacco <\s>
<s> and one fine day of june riding thither with the officer who visited the outposts colonel esmond was taking an airing on horseback being too weak for military duty they came to this river where a number of english and scots were assembled talking to the good natured enemy on the other side <\s>
<s> esmond was especially amused with the talk of one long fellow with a great curling red moustache and blue eyes that was half a dozen inches taller than his swarthy little comrades on the french side of the stream and being asked by the colonel saluted him and said that he belonged to the royal cravats <\s>
<s> from his way of saying royal cravat esmond at once knew that the fellow's tongue had first wagged on the banks of the liffey and not the loire and the poor soldier a deserter probably did not like to venture very deep into french conversation lest his unlucky brogue should peep out <\s>
<s> he chose to restrict himself to such few expressions in the french language as he thought he had mastered easily and his attempt at disguise was infinitely amusing <\s>
<s> esmond whistled lillibullero at which teague's eyes began to twinkle and then flung him a dollar when the poor boy broke out with a god bless that is dieu benisse votre honor that would infallibly have sent him to the provost marshal had he been on our side of the river <\s>
<s> whilst this parley was going on three officers on horseback on the french side appeared at some little distance and stopped as if eying us when one of them left the other two and rode close up to us who were by the stream <\s>
<s> says the royal cravat with great agitation pas lui that's he not him l'autre and pointed to the distant officer on a chestnut horse with a cuirass shining in the sun and over it a broad blue ribbon <\s>
<s> please to take mr <\s>
<s> hamilton's services to my lord marlborough my lord duke says the gentleman in english and looking to see that the party were not hostilely disposed he added with a smile there's a friend of yours gentlemen yonder he bids me to say that he saw some of your faces on the 11th of september last year <\s>
<s> as the gentleman spoke the other two officers rode up and came quite close <\s>
<s> we knew at once who it was <\s>
<s> it was the king then two and twenty years old tall and slim with deep brown eyes that looked melancholy though his lips wore a smile <\s>
<s> we took off our hats and saluted him <\s>
<s> no man sure could see for the first time without emotion the youthful inheritor of so much fame and misfortune <\s>

<s> the officer in whose company esmond was the same little captain of handyside's regiment mr <\s>

<s> last year his grace had been all for the whigs and hanoverians but finding on going to england his country cold towards himself and the people in a ferment of high church loyalty the duke comes back to his army cooled towards the hanoverians cautious with the imperialists and particularly civil and polite towards the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> tis certain that messengers and letters were continually passing between his grace and his brave nephew the duke of berwick in the opposite camp <\s>
<s> no man's caresses were more opportune than his grace's and no man ever uttered expressions of regard and affection more generously <\s>
<s> he professed to monsieur de torcy so mr <\s>
<s> john told the writer quite an eagerness to be cut in pieces for the exiled queen and her family nay more i believe this year he parted with a portion of the most precious part of himself his money which he sent over to the royal exiles <\s>
<s> tunstal who was in the prince's service was twice or thrice in and out of our camp the french in theirs of arlieu and about arras <\s>
<s> a little river the canihe i think twas called but this is writ away from books and europe and the only map the writer hath of these scenes of his youth bears no mark of this little stream divided our pickets from the enemy's <\s>
<s> our sentries talked across the stream when they could make themselves understood to each other and when they could not grinned and handed each other their brandy flasks or their pouches of tobacco <\s>
<s> and one fine day of june riding thither with the officer who visited the outposts colonel esmond was taking an airing on horseback being too weak for military duty they came to this river where a number of english and scots were assembled talking to the good natured enemy on the other side <\s>
<s> esmond was especially amused with the talk of one long fellow with a great curling red moustache and blue eyes that was half a dozen inches taller than his swarthy little comrades on the french side of the stream and being asked by the colonel saluted him and said that he belonged to the royal cravats <\s>
<s> from his way of saying royal cravat esmond at once knew that the fellow's tongue had first wagged on the banks of the liffey and not the loire and the poor soldier a deserter probably did not like to venture very deep into french conversation lest his unlucky brogue should peep out <\s>
<s> he chose to restrict himself to such few expressions in the french language as he thought he had mastered easily and his attempt at disguise was infinitely amusing <\s>
<s> esmond whistled lillibullero at which teague's eyes began to twinkle and then flung him a dollar when the poor boy broke out with a god bless that is dieu benisse votre honor that would infallibly have sent him to the provost marshal had he been on our side of the river <\s>
<s> whilst this parley was going on three officers on horseback on the french side appeared at some little distance and stopped as if eying us when one of them left the other two and rode close up to us who were by the stream <\s>
<s> says the royal cravat with great agitation pas lui that's he not him l'autre and pointed to the distant officer on a chestnut horse with a cuirass shining in the sun and over it a broad blue ribbon <\s>
<s> please to take mr <\s>
<s> hamilton's services to my lord marlborough my lord duke says the gentleman in english and looking to see that the party were not hostilely disposed he added with a smile there's a friend of yours gentlemen yonder he bids me to say that he saw some of your faces on the 11th of september last year <\s>
<s> as the gentleman spoke the other two officers rode up and came quite close <\s>
<s> we knew at once who it was <\s>
<s> it was the king then two and twenty years old tall and slim with deep brown eyes that looked melancholy though his lips wore a smile <\s>
<s> we took off our hats and saluted him <\s>
<s> no man sure could see for the first time without emotion the youthful inheritor of so much fame and misfortune <\s>
<s> it seemed to mr <\s>
<s> esmond that the prince was not unlike young castlewood whose age and figure he resembled <\s>
<s> the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george acknowledged the salute and looked at us hard <\s>
<s> even the idlers on our side of the river set up a hurrah <\s>
<s> as for the royal cravat he ran to the prince's stirrup knelt down and kissed his boot and bawled and looked a hundred ejaculations and blessings <\s>
<s> the prince bade the aide de camp give him a piece of money and when the party saluting us had ridden away cravat spat upon the piece of gold by way of benediction and swaggered away pouching his coin and twirling his honest carroty moustache <\s>
<s> the officer in whose company esmond was the same little captain of handyside's regiment mr <\s>
<s> sterne who had proposed the garden at lille when my lord mohun and esmond had their affair was an irishman too and as brave a little soul as ever wore a sword <\s>
<s> bedad says roger sterne that long fellow spoke french so beautiful that i shouldn't have known he wasn't a foreigner till he broke out with his hulla ballooing and only an irish calf can bellow like that <\s>
<s> and roger made another remark in his wild way in which there was sense as well as absurdity if that young gentleman says he would but ride over to our camp instead of villars's toss up his hat and say here am i the king who'll follow me <\s>
<s> by the lord esmond the whole army would rise and carry him home again and beat villars and take paris by the way <\s>
<s> the news of the prince's visit was all through the camp quickly and scores of ours went down in hopes to see him <\s>
<s> major hamilton whom we had talked with sent back by a trumpet several silver pieces for officers with us <\s>
<s> esmond received one of these and that medal and a recompense not uncommon amongst princes were the only rewards he ever had from a royal person whom he endeavored not very long after to serve <\s>
<s> esmond quitted the army almost immediately after this following his general home and indeed being advised to travel in the fine weather and attempt to take no further part in the campaign <\s>
<s> but he heard from the army that of the many who crowded to see the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george frank castlewood had made himself most conspicuous my lord viscount riding across the little stream bareheaded to where the prince was and dismounting and kneeling before him to do him homage <\s>
<s> some said that the prince had actually knighted him but my lord denied that statement though he acknowledged the rest of the story and said from having been out of favor with corporal john as he called the duke before his grace warned him not to commit those follies and smiled on him cordially ever after <\s>
<s> and he was so kind to me frank writ that i thought i would put in a good word for master harry but when i mentioned your name he looked as black as thunder and said he had never heard of you <\s>
<s> i go home and harp on the old string <\s>
<s> after quitting mons and the army and as he was waiting for a packet at ostend esmond had a letter from his young kinsman castlewood at bruxelles conveying intelligence whereof frank besought him to be the bearer to london and which caused colonel esmond no small anxiety <\s>
<s> the young scapegrace being one and twenty years old and being anxious to sow his wild otes as he wrote had married mademoiselle de wertheim daughter of count de wertheim chamberlain to the emperor and having a post in the household of the governor of the netherlands <\s>
<s> p s the young gentleman wrote clotilda is older than me which perhaps may be objected to her but i am so old a raik that the age makes no difference and i am determined to reform <\s>
<s> we were married at st <\s>
<s> gudule by father holt <\s>
<s> she is heart and soul for the good cause <\s>
<s> and here the cry is vif le roy which my mother will join in and trix too <\s>
<s> break this news to em gently and tell mr <\s>
<s> finch my agent to press the people for their rents and send me the ryno anyhow <\s>
<s> clotilda sings and plays on the spinet beautifully <\s>
<s> she is a fair beauty <\s>
<s> and if it's a son you shall stand godfather <\s>
<s> i'm going to leave the army having had enuf of soldering and my lord duke recommends me <\s>
<s> i shall pass the winter here and stop at least until clo's lying in <\s>
<s> i call her old clo but nobody else shall <\s>
<s> she is the cleverest woman in all bruxelles understanding painting music poetry and perfect at cookery and puddens <\s>
<s> i borded with the count that's how i came to know her <\s>
<s> there are four counts her brothers <\s>
<s> one an abbey three with the prince's army <\s>
<s> they have a lawsuit for an immence fortune but are now in a pore way <\s>

<s> and write and bid finch write amediately <\s>
<s> hostel de l'aigle noire bruxelles flanders <\s>
<s> so frank had married a roman catholic lady and an heir was expected and mr <\s>
<s> esmond was to carry this intelligence to his mistress at london <\s>
<s> twas a difficult embassy and the colonel felt not a little tremor as he neared the capital <\s>
<s> he reached his inn late and sent a messenger to kensington to announce his arrival and visit the next morning <\s>
<s> the messenger brought back news that the court was at windsor and the fair beatrix absent and engaged in her duties there <\s>
<s> only esmond's mistress remained in her house at kensington <\s>
<s> she appeared in court but once in the year beatrix was quite the mistress and ruler of the little mansion inviting the company thither and engaging in every conceivable frolic of town pleasure <\s>
<s> whilst her mother acting as the young lady's protectress and elder sister pursued her own path which was quite modest and secluded <\s>
<s> as soon as ever esmond was dressed and he had been awake long before the town he took a coach for kensington and reached it so early that he met his dear mistress coming home from morning prayers <\s>
<s> she carried her prayer book never allowing a footman to bear it as everybody else did and it was by this simple sign esmond knew what her occupation had been <\s>
<s> he called to the coachman to stop and jumped out as she looked towards him <\s>
<s> she wore her hood as usual and she turned quite pale when she saw him <\s>
<s> to feel that kind little hand near to his heart seemed to give him strength <\s>
<s> they were soon at the door of her ladyship's house and within it <\s>
<s> with a sweet sad smile she took his hand and kissed it <\s>
<s> how ill you have been how weak you look my dear henry she said <\s>
<s> tis certain the colonel did look like a ghost except that ghosts do not look very happy tis said <\s>
<s> esmond always felt so on returning to her after absence indeed whenever he looked in her sweet kind face <\s>
<s> i am come back to be nursed by my family says he <\s>
<s> if frank had not taken care of me after my wound very likely i should have gone altogether <\s>
<s> poor frank good frank <\s>
<s> you'll always be kind to him my lord she went on <\s>
<s> the poor child never knew he was doing you a wrong <\s>

<s> bedad says roger sterne that long fellow spoke french so beautiful that i shouldn't have known he wasn't a foreigner till he broke out with his hulla ballooing and only an irish calf can bellow like that <\s>
<s> and roger made another remark in his wild way in which there was sense as well as absurdity if that young gentleman says he would but ride over to our camp instead of villars's toss up his hat and say here am i the king who'll follow me <\s>
<s> by the lord esmond the whole army would rise and carry him home again and beat villars and take paris by the way <\s>
<s> the news of the prince's visit was all through the camp quickly and scores of ours went down in hopes to see him <\s>
<s> major hamilton whom we had talked with sent back by a trumpet several silver pieces for officers with us <\s>
<s> esmond received one of these and that medal and a recompense not uncommon amongst princes were the only rewards he ever had from a royal person whom he endeavored not very long after to serve <\s>
<s> esmond quitted the army almost immediately after this following his general home and indeed being advised to travel in the fine weather and attempt to take no further part in the campaign <\s>
<s> but he heard from the army that of the many who crowded to see the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george frank castlewood had made himself most conspicuous my lord viscount riding across the little stream bareheaded to where the prince was and dismounting and kneeling before him to do him homage <\s>
<s> some said that the prince had actually knighted him but my lord denied that statement though he acknowledged the rest of the story and said from having been out of favor with corporal john as he called the duke before his grace warned him not to commit those follies and smiled on him cordially ever after <\s>
<s> and he was so kind to me frank writ that i thought i would put in a good word for master harry but when i mentioned your name he looked as black as thunder and said he had never heard of you <\s>
<s> i go home and harp on the old string <\s>
<s> after quitting mons and the army and as he was waiting for a packet at ostend esmond had a letter from his young kinsman castlewood at bruxelles conveying intelligence whereof frank besought him to be the bearer to london and which caused colonel esmond no small anxiety <\s>
<s> the young scapegrace being one and twenty years old and being anxious to sow his wild otes as he wrote had married mademoiselle de wertheim daughter of count de wertheim chamberlain to the emperor and having a post in the household of the governor of the netherlands <\s>
<s> p s the young gentleman wrote clotilda is older than me which perhaps may be objected to her but i am so old a raik that the age makes no difference and i am determined to reform <\s>
<s> we were married at st <\s>
<s> gudule by father holt <\s>
<s> she is heart and soul for the good cause <\s>
<s> and here the cry is vif le roy which my mother will join in and trix too <\s>

<s> finch my agent to press the people for their rents and send me the ryno anyhow <\s>

<s> she is a fair beauty <\s>
<s> and if it's a son you shall stand godfather <\s>
<s> i'm going to leave the army having had enuf of soldering and my lord duke recommends me <\s>
<s> i shall pass the winter here and stop at least until clo's lying in <\s>
<s> i call her old clo but nobody else shall <\s>
<s> she is the cleverest woman in all bruxelles understanding painting music poetry and perfect at cookery and puddens <\s>
<s> i borded with the count that's how i came to know her <\s>
<s> there are four counts her brothers <\s>
<s> one an abbey three with the prince's army <\s>

<s> hostel de l'aigle noire bruxelles flanders <\s>
<s> so frank had married a roman catholic lady and an heir was expected and mr <\s>
<s> esmond was to carry this intelligence to his mistress at london <\s>
<s> twas a difficult embassy and the colonel felt not a little tremor as he neared the capital <\s>
<s> he reached his inn late and sent a messenger to kensington to announce his arrival and visit the next morning <\s>
<s> the messenger brought back news that the court was at windsor and the fair beatrix absent and engaged in her duties there <\s>
<s> only esmond's mistress remained in her house at kensington <\s>
<s> she appeared in court but once in the year beatrix was quite the mistress and ruler of the little mansion inviting the company thither and engaging in every conceivable frolic of town pleasure <\s>
<s> whilst her mother acting as the young lady's protectress and elder sister pursued her own path which was quite modest and secluded <\s>
<s> as soon as ever esmond was dressed and he had been awake long before the town he took a coach for kensington and reached it so early that he met his dear mistress coming home from morning prayers <\s>
<s> she carried her prayer book never allowing a footman to bear it as everybody else did and it was by this simple sign esmond knew what her occupation had been <\s>
<s> he called to the coachman to stop and jumped out as she looked towards him <\s>
<s> she wore her hood as usual and she turned quite pale when she saw him <\s>
<s> to feel that kind little hand near to his heart seemed to give him strength <\s>
<s> they were soon at the door of her ladyship's house and within it <\s>
<s> with a sweet sad smile she took his hand and kissed it <\s>
<s> how ill you have been how weak you look my dear henry she said <\s>
<s> tis certain the colonel did look like a ghost except that ghosts do not look very happy tis said <\s>
<s> esmond always felt so on returning to her after absence indeed whenever he looked in her sweet kind face <\s>
<s> i am come back to be nursed by my family says he <\s>
<s> if frank had not taken care of me after my wound very likely i should have gone altogether <\s>
<s> poor frank good frank <\s>
<s> you'll always be kind to him my lord she went on <\s>
<s> the poor child never knew he was doing you a wrong <\s>
<s> cries out colonel esmond <\s>
<s> what do you mean dear lady <\s>
<s> i am no lady says she i am rachel esmond francis esmond's widow my lord <\s>
<s> i cannot bear that title <\s>
<s> would we never had taken it from him who has it now <\s>
<s> but we did all in our power henry we did all in our power and my lord and i that is who told you this tale dearest lady <\s>
<s> have you not had the letter i writ you <\s>
<s> i writ to you at mons directly i heard it says lady esmond <\s>
<s> he was come back a greater jacobite than ever and esmond suspected that some fair conspirators at bruxelles had been inflaming the young man's ardor <\s>
<s> indeed he owned that he had a message from the queen beatrix's godmother who had given her name to frank's sister the year before he and his sovereign were born <\s>
<s> however desirous marshal villars might be to fight my lord duke did not seem disposed to indulge him this campaign <\s>
<s> last year his grace had been all for the whigs and hanoverians but finding on going to england his country cold towards himself and the people in a ferment of high church loyalty the duke comes back to his army cooled towards the hanoverians cautious with the imperialists and particularly civil and polite towards the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> tis certain that messengers and letters were continually passing between his grace and his brave nephew the duke of berwick in the opposite camp <\s>
<s> no man's caresses were more opportune than his grace's and no man ever uttered expressions of regard and affection more generously <\s>
<s> he professed to monsieur de torcy so mr <\s>
<s> john told the writer quite an eagerness to be cut in pieces for the exiled queen and her family nay more i believe this year he parted with a portion of the most precious part of himself his money which he sent over to the royal exiles <\s>
<s> tunstal who was in the prince's service was twice or thrice in and out of our camp the french in theirs of arlieu and about arras <\s>
<s> a little river the canihe i think twas called but this is writ away from books and europe and the only map the writer hath of these scenes of his youth bears no mark of this little stream divided our pickets from the enemy's <\s>
<s> our sentries talked across the stream when they could make themselves understood to each other and when they could not grinned and handed each other their brandy flasks or their pouches of tobacco <\s>
<s> and one fine day of june riding thither with the officer who visited the outposts colonel esmond was taking an airing on horseback being too weak for military duty they came to this river where a number of english and scots were assembled talking to the good natured enemy on the other side <\s>
<s> esmond was especially amused with the talk of one long fellow with a great curling red moustache and blue eyes that was half a dozen inches taller than his swarthy little comrades on the french side of the stream and being asked by the colonel saluted him and said that he belonged to the royal cravats <\s>
<s> from his way of saying royal cravat esmond at once knew that the fellow's tongue had first wagged on the banks of the liffey and not the loire and the poor soldier a deserter probably did not like to venture very deep into french conversation lest his unlucky brogue should peep out <\s>
<s> he chose to restrict himself to such few expressions in the french language as he thought he had mastered easily and his attempt at disguise was infinitely amusing <\s>
<s> esmond whistled lillibullero at which teague's eyes began to twinkle and then flung him a dollar when the poor boy broke out with a god bless that is dieu benisse votre honor that would infallibly have sent him to the provost marshal had he been on our side of the river <\s>
<s> whilst this parley was going on three officers on horseback on the french side appeared at some little distance and stopped as if eying us when one of them left the other two and rode close up to us who were by the stream <\s>
<s> says the royal cravat with great agitation pas lui that's he not him l'autre and pointed to the distant officer on a chestnut horse with a cuirass shining in the sun and over it a broad blue ribbon <\s>
<s> please to take mr <\s>
<s> hamilton's services to my lord marlborough my lord duke says the gentleman in english and looking to see that the party were not hostilely disposed he added with a smile there's a friend of yours gentlemen yonder he bids me to say that he saw some of your faces on the 11th of september last year <\s>
<s> as the gentleman spoke the other two officers rode up and came quite close <\s>
<s> we knew at once who it was <\s>
<s> it was the king then two and twenty years old tall and slim with deep brown eyes that looked melancholy though his lips wore a smile <\s>

<s> she appeared in court but once in the year beatrix was quite the mistress and ruler of the little mansion inviting the company thither and engaging in every conceivable frolic of town pleasure <\s>
<s> whilst her mother acting as the young lady's protectress and elder sister pursued her own path which was quite modest and secluded <\s>
<s> as soon as ever esmond was dressed and he had been awake long before the town he took a coach for kensington and reached it so early that he met his dear mistress coming home from morning prayers <\s>
<s> she carried her prayer book never allowing a footman to bear it as everybody else did and it was by this simple sign esmond knew what her occupation had been <\s>
<s> he called to the coachman to stop and jumped out as she looked towards him <\s>
<s> she wore her hood as usual and she turned quite pale when she saw him <\s>
<s> to feel that kind little hand near to his heart seemed to give him strength <\s>
<s> they were soon at the door of her ladyship's house and within it <\s>
<s> with a sweet sad smile she took his hand and kissed it <\s>
<s> how ill you have been how weak you look my dear henry she said <\s>
<s> tis certain the colonel did look like a ghost except that ghosts do not look very happy tis said <\s>
<s> esmond always felt so on returning to her after absence indeed whenever he looked in her sweet kind face <\s>
<s> i am come back to be nursed by my family says he <\s>
<s> if frank had not taken care of me after my wound very likely i should have gone altogether <\s>
<s> poor frank good frank <\s>
<s> you'll always be kind to him my lord she went on <\s>
<s> the poor child never knew he was doing you a wrong <\s>
<s> cries out colonel esmond <\s>
<s> what do you mean dear lady <\s>
<s> i am no lady says she i am rachel esmond francis esmond's widow my lord <\s>
<s> i cannot bear that title <\s>
<s> would we never had taken it from him who has it now <\s>
<s> but we did all in our power henry we did all in our power and my lord and i that is who told you this tale dearest lady <\s>
<s> have you not had the letter i writ you <\s>
<s> i writ to you at mons directly i heard it says lady esmond <\s>
<s> he was come back a greater jacobite than ever and esmond suspected that some fair conspirators at bruxelles had been inflaming the young man's ardor <\s>
<s> indeed he owned that he had a message from the queen beatrix's godmother who had given her name to frank's sister the year before he and his sovereign were born <\s>
<s> however desirous marshal villars might be to fight my lord duke did not seem disposed to indulge him this campaign <\s>
<s> last year his grace had been all for the whigs and hanoverians but finding on going to england his country cold towards himself and the people in a ferment of high church loyalty the duke comes back to his army cooled towards the hanoverians cautious with the imperialists and particularly civil and polite towards the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> tis certain that messengers and letters were continually passing between his grace and his brave nephew the duke of berwick in the opposite camp <\s>
<s> no man's caresses were more opportune than his grace's and no man ever uttered expressions of regard and affection more generously <\s>
<s> he professed to monsieur de torcy so mr <\s>
<s> john told the writer quite an eagerness to be cut in pieces for the exiled queen and her family nay more i believe this year he parted with a portion of the most precious part of himself his money which he sent over to the royal exiles <\s>
<s> tunstal who was in the prince's service was twice or thrice in and out of our camp the french in theirs of arlieu and about arras <\s>
<s> a little river the canihe i think twas called but this is writ away from books and europe and the only map the writer hath of these scenes of his youth bears no mark of this little stream divided our pickets from the enemy's <\s>
<s> our sentries talked across the stream when they could make themselves understood to each other and when they could not grinned and handed each other their brandy flasks or their pouches of tobacco <\s>
<s> and one fine day of june riding thither with the officer who visited the outposts colonel esmond was taking an airing on horseback being too weak for military duty they came to this river where a number of english and scots were assembled talking to the good natured enemy on the other side <\s>
<s> esmond was especially amused with the talk of one long fellow with a great curling red moustache and blue eyes that was half a dozen inches taller than his swarthy little comrades on the french side of the stream and being asked by the colonel saluted him and said that he belonged to the royal cravats <\s>
<s> from his way of saying royal cravat esmond at once knew that the fellow's tongue had first wagged on the banks of the liffey and not the loire and the poor soldier a deserter probably did not like to venture very deep into french conversation lest his unlucky brogue should peep out <\s>
<s> he chose to restrict himself to such few expressions in the french language as he thought he had mastered easily and his attempt at disguise was infinitely amusing <\s>
<s> esmond whistled lillibullero at which teague's eyes began to twinkle and then flung him a dollar when the poor boy broke out with a god bless that is dieu benisse votre honor that would infallibly have sent him to the provost marshal had he been on our side of the river <\s>
<s> whilst this parley was going on three officers on horseback on the french side appeared at some little distance and stopped as if eying us when one of them left the other two and rode close up to us who were by the stream <\s>
<s> says the royal cravat with great agitation pas lui that's he not him l'autre and pointed to the distant officer on a chestnut horse with a cuirass shining in the sun and over it a broad blue ribbon <\s>
<s> please to take mr <\s>
<s> hamilton's services to my lord marlborough my lord duke says the gentleman in english and looking to see that the party were not hostilely disposed he added with a smile there's a friend of yours gentlemen yonder he bids me to say that he saw some of your faces on the 11th of september last year <\s>
<s> as the gentleman spoke the other two officers rode up and came quite close <\s>
<s> we knew at once who it was <\s>
<s> it was the king then two and twenty years old tall and slim with deep brown eyes that looked melancholy though his lips wore a smile <\s>
<s> we took off our hats and saluted him <\s>
<s> no man sure could see for the first time without emotion the youthful inheritor of so much fame and misfortune <\s>
<s> it seemed to mr <\s>
<s> esmond that the prince was not unlike young castlewood whose age and figure he resembled <\s>
<s> the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george acknowledged the salute and looked at us hard <\s>
<s> even the idlers on our side of the river set up a hurrah <\s>
<s> as for the royal cravat he ran to the prince's stirrup knelt down and kissed his boot and bawled and looked a hundred ejaculations and blessings <\s>
<s> the prince bade the aide de camp give him a piece of money and when the party saluting us had ridden away cravat spat upon the piece of gold by way of benediction and swaggered away pouching his coin and twirling his honest carroty moustache <\s>
<s> the officer in whose company esmond was the same little captain of handyside's regiment mr <\s>
<s> sterne who had proposed the garden at lille when my lord mohun and esmond had their affair was an irishman too and as brave a little soul as ever wore a sword <\s>
<s> bedad says roger sterne that long fellow spoke french so beautiful that i shouldn't have known he wasn't a foreigner till he broke out with his hulla ballooing and only an irish calf can bellow like that <\s>
<s> and roger made another remark in his wild way in which there was sense as well as absurdity if that young gentleman says he would but ride over to our camp instead of villars's toss up his hat and say here am i the king who'll follow me <\s>
<s> by the lord esmond the whole army would rise and carry him home again and beat villars and take paris by the way <\s>
<s> the news of the prince's visit was all through the camp quickly and scores of ours went down in hopes to see him <\s>
<s> major hamilton whom we had talked with sent back by a trumpet several silver pieces for officers with us <\s>
<s> esmond received one of these and that medal and a recompense not uncommon amongst princes were the only rewards he ever had from a royal person whom he endeavored not very long after to serve <\s>
<s> esmond quitted the army almost immediately after this following his general home and indeed being advised to travel in the fine weather and attempt to take no further part in the campaign <\s>
<s> but he heard from the army that of the many who crowded to see the chevalier de st <\s>
<s> george frank castlewood had made himself most conspicuous my lord viscount riding across the little stream bareheaded to where the prince was and dismounting and kneeling before him to do him homage <\s>
<s> some said that the prince had actually knighted him but my lord denied that statement though he acknowledged the rest of the story and said from having been out of favor with corporal john as he called the duke before his grace warned him not to commit those follies and smiled on him cordially ever after <\s>
<s> and he was so kind to me frank writ that i thought i would put in a good word for master harry but when i mentioned your name he looked as black as thunder and said he had never heard of you <\s>
<s> i go home and harp on the old string <\s>
<s> after quitting mons and the army and as he was waiting for a packet at ostend esmond had a letter from his young kinsman castlewood at bruxelles conveying intelligence whereof frank besought him to be the bearer to london and which caused colonel esmond no small anxiety <\s>
<s> the young scapegrace being one and twenty years old and being anxious to sow his wild otes as he wrote had married mademoiselle de wertheim daughter of count de wertheim chamberlain to the emperor and having a post in the household of the governor of the netherlands <\s>
